
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Analyze the geometric configuration of the torus generated by revolving a circle of radius 3 around an axis 6 units from its center.'}, {'objective': 'Determine the radius of the tangent circle when the torus rests externally tangent to the sphere of radius 11 in the first orientation.'}, {'objective': 'Determine the radius of the tangent circle when the torus rests externally tangent to the sphere of radius 11 in the second orientation.'}, {'objective': 'Calculate the difference between the two tangent circle radii, express it as a simplified fraction, and return the sum of numerator and denominator.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- The torus T is generated by revolving a circle of radius 3 around an axis in the plane of the circle, with the axis located 6 units from the circle's center. This creates a standard torus with major radius R = 6 and minor radius r = 3.
- The sphere S has radius 11.
- The torus T is placed externally tangent to the sphere S in two different ways, each time tangent along a circle on the torus surface.
- These two tangency circles have radii r_i and r_o respectively.
- The problem asks for the difference r_i - r_o expressed as a reduced fraction m/n, and then to find m + n.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The torus is defined by two radii: the major radius (distance from the center of the tube to the axis of revolution) and the minor radius (radius of the tube).
- The sphere and torus are externally tangent, meaning they touch but do not intersect, and the contact is along a circle on the torus.
- The two different tangency configurations correspond to the torus resting on the sphere in two distinct ways, producing two different circles of tangency with radii r_i and r_o.
- The difference r_i - r_o involves understanding how the geometry of the torus and sphere interact, likely involving distances between centers and radii, and the geometry of the circles formed by intersection or tangency.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in geometry, specifically 3D geometry involving surfaces of revolution.
- Concepts from differential geometry or classical Euclidean geometry of surfaces may be relevant.
- The problem is typical of mathematical competitions or advanced geometry problems.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The problem states "when T rests on the outside of S" twice, which may be a typographical repetition; presumably, one configuration corresponds to the torus resting on the sphere in one orientation, and the other in a different orientation.
- The exact positions or orientations of the torus relative to the sphere are not explicitly given, so assumptions about alignment and contact points may be necessary.
- The meaning of "circle with radius r_i" and "circle with radius r_o" refers to the radius of the circle of tangency on the torus surface, but the problem does not specify which is inner or outer; the subscripts suggest inner and outer.
- It may be necessary to assume standard positioning (e.g., both centered along the same axis) to analyze the problem.
- The problem involves understanding the geometry of the torus and sphere in contact, which can be complex; careful geometric reasoning or algebraic modeling is needed.

    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Formally define the torus T by specifying its major radius R and minor radius r based on the given circle radius and axis distance, and represent the sphere S with its radius.     cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)

    debate_agents_7 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in self.debate_role]

        "context": ["user query", thinking6.content, answer6.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }
    for r in range(N_max_7):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_7):
            if r == 0:
                thinking7, answer7 = await agent([taskInfo, thinking6, answer6], debate_instruction_7, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_7 = [taskInfo, thinking6, answer6] + all_thinking7[r-1] + all_answer7[r-1]
                thinking7, answer7 = await agent(input_infos_7, debate_instruction_7, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, verifying difference, thinking: {thinking7.content}; answer: {answer7.content}")
            all_thinking7[r].append(thinking7)

    final_decision_agent_7 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)

    cot_reflect_instruction_8 = "Sub-task 8: Compute the final answer m + n from the simplified fraction m/n representing r_i - r_o, and summarize the solution clearly." + reflect_inst_8
    cot_agent_8 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_8 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_8 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_8 = [taskInfo, thinking7, answer7]
    subtask_desc8 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_8",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_8,
        "context": ["user query", thinking7.content, answer7.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking8, answer8 = await cot_agent_8(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_8.id}, computing final answer m+n, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_8):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_8([taskInfo, thinking8, answer8], "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_8.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_8.extend([thinking8, answer8, feedback])
        thinking8, answer8 = await cot_agent_8(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_8.id}, refining final answer m+n, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 8 output: thinking - {thinking8.content}; answer - {answer8.content}")
    subtask_desc8['response'] = {"thinking": thinking8, "answer": answer8}
    logs.append(subtask_desc8)

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking8, answer8, sub_tasks, agents)
    for i, step in enumerate(sub_tasks, 1):
        print(f"Step {i}: ", step)
    return final_answer, logs

The torus is tangent externally to the sphere in two configurations, each tangent along a circle on the torus with radii r_i and r_o. The difference r_i - r_o can be expressed as a simplified fraction m/n. From the geometry, the radii of the tangent circles on the torus are r_i = 6 - sqrt(9 - h^2) and r_o = 6 + sqrt(9 - h^2), where h is the height at which the tangency occurs. async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Formally define the torus T by specifying its major radius R and minor radius r based on the given circle radius and axis distance. Represent the sphere S with its radius. Clearly state the coordinate system and assumptions about the relative positioning and orientation of T and S to enable precise geometric analysis. Avoid making assumptions about tangency positions at this stage."
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, defining torus and sphere parameters, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking1, "answer": answer1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc1)

    cot_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Express the geometric conditions for external tangency between the torus T and the sphere S, focusing on the constraints that define the circle of tangency on the torus surface. Formulate these conditions separately for the two distinct tangency configurations without attempting to solve them yet. Avoid conflating the two cases or assuming identical parameters."
    cot_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1.content, answer1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agent_2([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], cot_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_2.id}, formulating tangency conditions, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking2, "answer": answer2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc2)

    N = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_3 = []
    possible_thinkings_3 = []
    subtask_desc3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_3",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking2.content, answer2.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N):
        thinking3, answer3 = await cot_agents_3[i]([taskInfo, thinking2, answer2], cot_sc_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_3[i].id}, clarifying radii relations, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
        possible_answers_3.append(answer3)
        possible_thinkings_3.append(thinking3)
    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo] + possible_answers_3 + possible_thinkings_3, "Sub-task 3: Synthesize and choose the most consistent clarification for radii r_i and r_o.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking3, "answer": answer3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc3)

                input_infos_9 = [taskInfo, thinking8, answer8] + all_thinking9[r-1] + all_answer9[r-1]
                thinking9, answer9 = await agent(input_infos_9, debate_instruction_9, r, is_sub_task=True)

    cot_reflect_instruction_10 = "Sub-task 10: Compute the final answer m + n from the simplified fraction m/n representing r_i - r_o. Summarize the entire solution clearly, including key steps and final result. Ensure the answer is consistent with all prior verified results." + reflect_inst_10

    critic_agent_10 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_10 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_10 = [taskInfo, thinking9, answer9]
    subtask_desc10 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_10",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_10,
        "context": ["user query", thinking9.content, answer9.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking10, answer10 = await cot_agent_10(cot_inputs_10, cot_reflect_instruction_10, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_10.id}, computing final answer, thinking: {thinking10.content}; answer: {answer10.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_10):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_10([taskInfo, thinking10, answer10], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_10.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_10.extend([thinking10, answer10, feedback])
        thinking10, answer10 = await cot_agent_10(cot_inputs_10, cot_reflect_instruction_10, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_10.id}, refining final answer, thinking: {thinking10.content}; answer: {answer10.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 10 output: thinking - {thinking10.content}; answer - {answer10.content}")
    subtask_desc10['response'] = {"thinking": thinking10, "answer": answer10}
    logs.append(subtask_desc10)

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking10, answer10, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs
